INC-SOURCE (SPALL) The maximum neutron flight distance of Back-n  3291300100027 
           is approximately 80 m, while the neutron energy range  3291300100028 
           is 0.5 eV-200 MeV. At the Back-n experimental station, 3291300100029 
            the neutron flux can reach 10E7 /cm2s1.               3291300100030 
SAMPLE     (47-AG-107,ENR=0.995) The 107Ag sample with diameter   3291300100031 
           of 30.000+-0.001 mm, thickness of 0.100+-0.001 mm and  3291300100032 
           weight of 0.745+-0.005 g. The present 107Ag sample     3291300100033 
           contains 0.3% 109Ag impurity.                          3291300100034 
DETECTOR   (SCIN) A detection system consisting of four C6D6      3291300100035 
           scintillation detectors, approximately 76 m away from  3291300100036 
           the spallation target. Each C6D6 liquid scintillator   3291300100037 
           has 127 mm in diameter and 76.2 mm in length, and the  3291300100038 
           scintillator was contained in a 1.5-mm thick aluminum  3291300100039 
           capsule and coupled with a photomultiplier tube (ETEL  3291300100040 
           9390 KEB PMT).                                         3291300100041 
           (SILI) The neutron flux was measured by a Li-Si        3291300100042 
           detector, which is based on the 6Li(n,a) 3H reaction.  3291300100043 
METHOD     (TOF,PHWT) Flight distance is approximately 76 m. The  3291300100044 
           experiment took about 57.5 h.                          3291300100045 
CORRECTION Corrected for neutron multiple scattering with GEANT4  3291300100046
